## Task 14.1: Fix undefined _blob reference in ParamAlias rest client generation (2026-03-05)

**Problem**: When `@paramAlias("blob")` is applied to a client initialization parameter `blobName`, the RestClient generates `_blob` (the alias) instead of `_blobName` (the actual client field) in request builder methods. This causes CS0103 compilation errors.

**Root cause**: `buildPathParamStatement`, `buildQueryParamStatement`, and `buildHeaderParamStatement` in `RestClientFile.tsx` constructed onClient field names as `_${getParamName(param.name)}`, but `param.name` is the operation-level alias, not the client initialization parameter name.

**Fix**: Added `getOnClientFieldName()` helper that uses `param.correspondingMethodParams[0].name` to resolve the correct client initialization parameter name. Applied the helper in all three build functions.

**Files changed**:
- `src/components/clients/RestClientFile.tsx` ŌĆö added `getOnClientFieldName()`, updated 3 build functions
- `test/rest-client.test.ts` ŌĆö added unit test verifying correct field name resolution for @paramAlias

**Patterns**: For onClient params, always use `correspondingMethodParams` to get the field name, never `param.name` directly. This handles both aliased and non-aliased parameters correctly.

**E2E result**: client-initialization/default, individually, and individuallyParent all pass (Ō£ģ 12/111, 13/111, 16/111).

2026-03-05 ŌĆö Task 14.2: Fix undefined Argument helper class in generated model constructors

Problem: Models in cross-namespace scenarios (e.g., Azure.Core.Foundations vs root namespace _Specs_.Azure.Core.Lro.Rpc) referenced Argument.AssertNotNull() as a raw string. Since Argument is in the root namespace and models are in different namespaces, C# couldn't resolve the reference without a using directive.

Solution: Used Alloy's refkey mechanism for automatic cross-namespace using generation:
1. Added argumentRefkey() to src/utils/refkey.ts using Symbol.for("http-client-csharp:argument")
2. Registered the refkey on ClassDeclaration in ArgumentFile.tsx
3. Changed buildNullChecks() in ModelConstructors.tsx to return Children[] (code template results) instead of string[], using code`${argumentRefkey()}.AssertNotNull(...)` instead of raw strings
4. Added renderPublicCtorBody() helper to assemble null checks (JSX) and assignments (strings) as mixed JSX children

Key pattern: When an infrastructure class (like Argument) is referenced from files in different namespaces, use a refkey + code template so Alloy auto-generates the using directive. Raw strings bypass Alloy's namespace resolution.

Files changed: src/utils/refkey.ts, src/components/infrastructure/ArgumentFile.tsx, src/components/models/ModelConstructors.tsx

## Task 14.3 ŌĆö Fix readonly field assignment error in model serialization constructors (2026-03-05)

**Problem:** Non-discriminated derived models (e.g., Cat : Pet, OuterModel : BaseModel) generated constructors that:
1. Didn't chain to `: base(...)` ŌĆö both public and serialization constructors
2. Didn't include inherited parameters (e.g., Cat's constructor lacked `name` from Pet)
3. Directly assigned `_additionalBinaryDataProperties` which is `private protected readonly` in the base class ŌåÆ CS0191

**Root Cause:** `ModelConstructors` only routed discriminated derived models (`isDerivedDiscriminatedModel`) to `DerivedModelConstructors`. Non-discriminated derived models fell through to `BaseModelConstructors` which generates standalone constructors without `: base(...)` chaining.

**Solution:** Generalized derived model constructor handling to cover both discriminated and non-discriminated inheritance:
1. Added `isDerivedModel(model)` function ŌĆö checks `model.baseModel !== undefined`
2. Updated routing in `ModelConstructors` to use `model.baseModel` check instead of `isDerivedDiscriminatedModel`
3. Updated `computePublicCtorParams` and `computeSerializationCtorParams` to handle non-discriminated derived models (recurse through base hierarchy)
4. Updated `DerivedModelConstructors` to handle both cases:
   - For discriminated: substitute discriminator literal in base call, validate ALL params (abstract base doesn't validate)
   - For non-discriminated: pass through all base params in base call, validate only OWN params (base validates its own)
5. Updated parallel functions in serialization files: `computeVariableInfos`, `computeMatchableProperties`, `computeAllXmlProperties`, `computeSerializationProperties`

**Key Pattern:** When `model.baseModel` is defined, the model is derived and needs `: base(...)` chaining regardless of whether it has a discriminator. The discriminator only affects HOW the base call is built (literal substitution vs pass-through).

**Files Changed:**
- `src/components/models/ModelConstructors.tsx` ŌĆö core fix
- `src/components/serialization/DeserializeVariableDeclarations.tsx`
- `src/components/serialization/PropertyMatchingLoop.tsx`
- `src/components/serialization/XmlDeserialize.tsx`
- `src/components/model-factory/ModelFactoryMethod.tsx`
- `test/scenarios/models/not_discriminated_inheritance.md` ŌĆö updated expectations

**Result:** 67 test files pass (1,304 tests), not-discriminated and access e2e scenarios compile without CS0191 errors

Both components already existed in `src/components/infrastructure/` but were not imported or rendered in the emitter output.    triggering `using System;`. The overrides use `System.TimeSpan`, `System.DateTimeOffset`,
   `System.Uri` refkeys which auto-generate the using directive.

2. **ConvenienceMethod.tsx** ŌĆö Fixed dict type handling in `getConvenienceTypeInfo()` to use
   `SystemCollectionsGeneric.IDictionary` refkey with `code` template (like arrays use
   `SystemCollectionsGeneric.IEnumerable`), instead of `<TypeExpression>` which rendered
   `IDictionary<string, T>` as a string without `using System.Collections.Generic;`.

3. **PropertyMatchingLoop.tsx** ŌĆö Replaced string literals `"List<"` and `"Dictionary<string, "`
   in deserialization code with `SystemCollectionsGeneric.List` and `SystemCollectionsGeneric.Dictionary`
   refkeys. Added `List` and `Dictionary` (concrete classes) to `system-collections-generic.ts` builtins.

**Specs fixed:**
- `type/dictionary` ŌĆö fully builds clean, removed from testignore
- `type/property/nullable` ŌĆö no more CS0246 errors (remaining CS7036 are unrelated)
- `payload/json-merge-patch` ŌĆö no more CS0246 errors (remaining CS7036 are unrelated)

  issues (not using directive issues), kept in testignore with updated comments.

- Modified: test/convenience-method.test.ts (added dict body param using directive test)

**Key design decision:**
- For types where the EF default produces the correct C# type name but as a string (not a refkey),
  we override them with the same type name via a refkey. This doesn't change the output text but
  ensures the using directive is auto-generated. This is the pattern for duration, utcDateTime,
  offsetDateTime, url.


## 2026-03-05 ŌĆö Task 12.21: Fix non-static member access in recursive model serialization

Fixed CS0120 errors in recursive model deserialization where a property name (PascalCase) shadows a type name in static methods.

**Root cause**: When `Element` has property `extension: Extension[]`, the PascalCase property `Extension` shadows the class `Extension` in static `DeserializeXxx()` methods. C# resolves `Extension.DeserializeExtension(...)` to the instance property, not the type.

**Fix**: Added `collectPropertyCSharpNames()` utility in `src/utils/property.ts` that collects all PascalCase property names from a model and its ancestors. When a model type name collides with a property name, the deserialization call uses a namespace-qualified type reference (e.g., `_Type.Model.Inheritance.Recursive.Extension.DeserializeExtension(...)`).

**Files changed**:
- `src/utils/property.ts` ŌĆö Added `collectPropertyCSharpNames()` utility
- `src/components/serialization/PropertyMatchingLoop.tsx` ŌĆö Threaded collision detection through `getReadExpression`, `renderArrayDeserialization`, `renderDictionaryDeserialization`
- `src/components/serialization/CastOperators.tsx` ŌĆö Added collision detection for explicit operator
- `test/model-serialization.test.ts` ŌĆö Updated 3 existing tests, added 1 new recursive model test
- `test/e2e/.testignore` ŌĆö Removed `type/model/inheritance/recursive`

**Key learning**: The C# naming policy context for PascalCase properties is `"class-property"`, not `"property"`. The `"property"` context falls through to camelCase. This distinction is critical for collision detection.

**Pattern**: This fix also applies to non-recursive models (e.g., `widget.pet: Pet` ŌåÆ `Pet` property shadows `Pet` type). The fix is general and handles all such cases.

## Task 12.23: Fix missing Argument helper class reference in LRO models (2026-03-05)

**Problem**: Extensible enums in cross-namespace scenarios (e.g., `OperationState` in `Azure.Core.Foundations`)
couldn't find the `Argument` helper class because the `using` directive for the root namespace was missing.
`ExtensibleEnumFile.tsx` and `LiteralTypeFile.tsx` used raw string `"Argument.AssertNotNull(...)"` which
prevented Alloy from auto-generating the `using` directive.

**Root Cause**: The extensible enum and literal type components generated `Argument.AssertNotNull` as raw
strings rather than using Alloy's refkey system. When the struct's namespace differed from the root
namespace, no `using` was generated for the Argument class's namespace.

**Fix**: Added `packageName` prop to `ExtensibleEnumFile` and `LiteralTypeFile` components, representing
the root namespace where `Argument` is declared. When the struct is in a namespace that is NOT the root
or a sub-namespace of it, a `using` directive is conditionally added. Namespace comparison uses
`useCSharpNamePolicy().getName(seg, "namespace")` to normalize casing (PascalCase) to match what
Alloy's `<Namespace>` component renders.

**Key learnings**:
- Using `argumentRefkey()` in a `code` template inside `SourceFile` causes self-referencing `using`
  directives (e.g., `using X;` inside `namespace X`). This is because Alloy adds auto-usings from
  refkeys but doesn't suppress self-referencing ones. Avoid using refkeys in components that manually
  manage usings as raw strings.
- C# automatically searches parent namespaces during name resolution, so sub-namespaces of the root
  DON'T need a `using` directive to find types in the root namespace.
- `resolveRootNamespace()` returns raw casing (may be lowercase), but `<Namespace>` applies PascalCase.
  Always normalize namespace strings via naming policy before using them in `using` directives.

**Files changed**:
- `src/components/enums/ExtensibleEnumFile.tsx` ŌĆö Added `packageName` prop, conditional `using` with namespace normalization
- `src/components/literal-types/LiteralTypeFile.tsx` ŌĆö Same fix
- `src/emitter.tsx` ŌĆö Pass `rootNamespace` as `packageName` to both components
- `test/e2e/.testignore` ŌĆö Removed `azure/core/lro/rpc` and `azure/core/lro/standard`

## Task 12.26 (2026-03-05): Fix spread parameter model constructor missing additionalBinaryDataProperties (DONE)

**Problem**: Spread body convenience methods constructed models via `new BodyType(param1, param2, ...)` without passing `additionalBinaryDataProperties` (serialization constructor's last param), causing CS7036 errors. Additionally, args were in priority-sorted order (required first) instead of model property definition order, which would cause CS1503 for models with interleaved required/optional properties.

**Fix**: Two changes in `ConvenienceMethod.tsx`:
1. Added `spreadBodyParamsInOrder` to `ConvenienceParamsResult` ŌĆö body params re-sorted by original index to recover model property order (matching serialization constructor).
2. In `buildSpreadProtocolCallExpr`, use `bodyParamsInModelOrder` for correct arg ordering and append `default` for `additionalBinaryDataProperties` (conditional on `spreadBodyType.kind === "model"` to skip non-model spread bodies like string).

**Key insight**: `isSpreadBody()` returns true for non-model types (e.g., string with `@body` decorator) due to reference inequality of type objects. The `default` addition must be conditional on model types.

**Test added**: `passes spread model args in model property order with default for additionalBinaryDataProperties` ŌĆö uses model with interleaved required/optional to validate both ordering and default parameter.

**Files changed**: `src/components/clients/ConvenienceMethod.tsx`, 4 scenario test files updated expectations.

## 2026-03-05 ŌĆö Task 12.24: Fix CS1501 errors in three specs

### What was done
- Fixed two distinct CS1501 root causes across client/overload, azure/core/traits, special-headers/conditional-request

### Fix 1: CreateRequestMethod name collision (client/overload)
- In RestClientFile.tsx, CreateRequestMethod used plain string `name={methodName}` for the <Method> component
- When two operations map to the same C# name (via @clientName), Alloy's name deduplication added `_2` suffix
- Protocol methods referenced the un-suffixed name via string interpolation, causing CS1501
- Fix: Use `namekey(methodName, { ignoreNameConflict: true })` since C# method overloading handles same-named methods with different signatures

### Fix 2: DateTimeOffset?.ToString("O") on nullable types (azure/core/traits, conditional-request)
- getParamValueExpression generated `name.ToString("O")` for datetime types
- Nullable<DateTimeOffset> lacks the ToString(string format) overload, causing CS1501
- Fix: Use `TypeFormatters.ConvertToString(name, SerializationFormat.DateTime_RFC3339)` which handles nullable via boxing

### Files changed
- src/components/clients/RestClientFile.tsx (both fixes)
- test/rest-client.test.ts (updated existing test, added 2 new tests)
- test/e2e/.testignore (removed 3 specs from skip list)

### Patterns used
- `namekey(name, { ignoreNameConflict: true })` for C# method overloading
- `TypeFormatters.ConvertToString(value, SerializationFormat.DateTime_RFC3339)` for nullable-safe datetime formatting

### E2E results
- 84 specs succeeded (up from 81), 0 failed, 36 skipped

## 2026-03-05 ŌĆö Task 12.25: Fix union type serialization and conversion methods

**Root cause**: `getVariantBaseKind()` in `CSharpTypeExpression.tsx` didn't handle TypeSpec `Enum` or `EnumMember` types. For unions of enums like `LR | UD`, variants had kind "Enum" which fell through to `return type.kind`. `isMultiTypeUnion()` then classified "Enum" as multi-type (not in "string"/"numeric"/"boolean"), incorrectly mapping to BinaryData.

**Fix**: Added Enum and EnumMember handling in `getVariantBaseKind()` ŌĆö string-backed enums return "string", numeric-backed return "numeric". This correctly classifies unions of homogeneous enums as single-type unions (extensible enums), matching the legacy emitter behavior.

**Files changed**:
- `src/components/CSharpTypeExpression.tsx` ŌĆö Added Enum/EnumMember handling in `getVariantBaseKind()`, updated JSDoc
- `test/type-expression.test.tsx` ŌĆö Added 3 tests: string-backed enum union, numeric-backed enum union, mixed-backing enum union

**Verification**: CS1929 and CS0029 errors for EnumsOnlyCases eliminated. Generated `EnumsOnlyCases` properties correctly typed as `EnumsOnlyCasesLr`/`EnumsOnlyCasesUd`. All 1337 unit tests + 5 e2e tests pass.

**Note**: type/union spec has 2 remaining pre-existing CS1503 errors in `ModelsOnly.cs` (convenience method passes string where BinaryData expected for Cat|Dog model union). Not related to this task.

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 12.20: Fix type mapping in serialization constructors for inherited models

### What was done
Fixed 6 distinct compilation errors across 7 specs (out of 8 listed in the task):

1. **Model factory argument order** (not-discriminated, nested-discriminator, hierarchy-building):
   - Root cause: `basePropertyCount` in `ModelFactoryMethod.tsx` used immediate parent's total property count instead of root model's. For multi-level inheritance (e.g., SiameseŌåÆCatŌåÆPet), `additionalBinaryDataProperties` was inserted at the wrong position.
   - Fix: Added `getRootModelPropertyCount()` helper that walks to the root ancestor. The `null` for additionalBinaryDataProperties is now always inserted after the root model's own properties.

2. **Enum discriminator Unknown model** (enum-discriminator):
   - Root cause: Unknown variant used `"unknown"` string literal for all enum discriminators, but fixed C# enums don't have string constructors.
   - Fix: Differentiated between fixed enums (pass through as-is, matching legacy emitter), extensible enums (`new EnumType("unknown")`), and string discriminators (`?? "unknown"`).

3. **Uri serialization** (deserialize-empty-string-as-null):
   - Root cause: `PropertySerializer.tsx` grouped `url` with `string` kinds, generating `writer.WriteStringValue(Uri)` but `Utf8JsonWriter` has no Uri overload.
   - Fix: Separated `url` handling with `valueTransform: (name) => \`\${name}.AbsoluteUri\`` to produce `writer.WriteStringValue(Url.AbsoluteUri)`.

4. **IReadOnlyDictionary type mismatch** (type/model/visibility):
   - Root cause: `DeserializeVariableDeclarations.tsx` and `ModelFactoryMethod.tsx` used raw `TypeExpression` for collection types, ignoring read-only flag. Constructor params used `IReadOnlyDictionary` but variables used `IDictionary`.
   - Fix: Both components now use `renderCollectionPropertyType(type, isPropertyReadOnly(p))` for collection types, matching constructor parameter types.

5. **Scalar body type wrapping** (type/scalar):
   - Root cause: `buildSpreadProtocolCallExpr` in `ConvenienceMethod.tsx` unconditionally wrapped all spread body types in `new Type(value)`, but C# primitives (bool, decimal) don't have constructors.
   - Fix: Added early return for non-model spread body types that uses `BinaryContentHelper.FromObject(value)` directly.

### Patterns used
- `getRootModelPropertyCount()` walks inheritance chain to find root property count
- `renderCollectionPropertyType()` reused for variable declarations (not just constructor params)
- `isFixed` flag on SdkEnumType distinguishes fixed vs extensible enums

### What the next person should know
- The `routes` spec still has errors (separate root cause ŌĆö route parameter expansion for complex types). Tracked in new task 12.28.
- The `isPropertyReadOnly` function from utils/property.ts is key for determining collection interface variant.
- Deserialization variable types must match constructor param types ŌĆö both now use the same rendering path for collections.

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 12.19: Add namespace collision detection for generated type names

### What was done
Fixed three types of namespace/type name collision errors affecting azure/example/basic, type/union/discriminated, and type/property/optionality specs.

### Root causes and fixes
1. **Literal type namespace bug (CS0118 Type)**: `collectLiteralTypes()` in emitter.tsx was called BEFORE `cleanAllNamespaces()`, so literal type wrapper structs captured uncleaned namespaces (e.g., `Type.Property.Optional` instead of `_Type.Property.Optional`). Fix: moved the call AFTER namespace cleaning.

2. **ModelFactory using System collision (CS0104 Enum)**: `ModelFactoryFile.tsx` explicitly added `using System;` via the SourceFile `using` prop, even though Alloy adds it automatically when needed via refkey resolution. This brought `System.Enum` into scope unnecessarily, colliding with generated `Enum` structs. Fix: removed `"System"` from explicit using list.

3. **Sub-client Object collision (CS0104 Object)**: Sub-client named "Object" was referenced via `refkey(child)` in ClientFile, rendering as short name `Object` which collides with `System.Object`. Fix: added `isSystemTypeNameCollision()` utility that detects well-known BCL type names; ClientFile now uses fully-qualified namespace paths for colliding sub-client references.

### Key patterns
- `isSystemTypeNameCollision()` in `src/utils/package-name.ts` ŌĆö checks type names against a set of known .NET BCL types
- FQN approach bypasses Alloy's short-name + `using` resolution to avoid ambiguity
- Literal type collection must happen AFTER namespace cleaning to capture cleaned namespaces

### Note for next iterations
- `type/property/optionality` has pre-existing literal type serialization errors (CS0103 _value, CS0266/CS1503 type conversion) unrelated to namespace collisions. These were masked by the CS0118 error.
- The `"System"` removal from ModelFactory works because Alloy adds `using System;` automatically when types from the System namespace are referenced via refkeys.

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 12.28: Fix convenience method parameter mapping for route parameter expansion

### Problem
Routes spec had 64 CS1503 compilation errors across two categories:
1. **RequestOptionsŌåÆCancellationToken (28 errors)**: Convenience methods with `IDictionary<string, int>` params called protocol methods with `string` params, causing overload resolution failure
2. **boolŌåÆSerializationFormat (8 errors)**: `AppendPathDelimited(param, ",", true)` passed `bool` as 3rd positional arg where `SerializationFormat` was expected

### Root Cause
`getProtocolTypeExpression()` in both ProtocolMethod.tsx and RestClientFile.tsx was missing a `case "dict"` handler. Dict types fell to `default ŌåÆ "string"`, but convenience methods correctly used `IDictionary<string, T>`.

### Fix (5 files modified)
1. **ProtocolMethod.tsx**: Added `case "dict"` ŌåÆ returns `IDictionary<string, T>` via refkey
2. **RestClientFile.tsx**: Added `case "dict"` to `getProtocolTypeExpression()`, added `isDictType()` helper, fixed `buildPathParamStatement()` to use named `escape:` arg and handle dict types, added dict handling to `buildQueryParamStatement()` for both exploded and non-exploded cases
3. **ClientUriBuilderFile.tsx**: Added dict overloads for `AppendPathDelimited` and `AppendQueryDelimited` that serialize key-value pairs as interleaved comma-delimited strings
4. **test/e2e/.testignore**: Removed routes from ignore list

### Tests added (5 new tests)
- protocol-method.test.ts: dict path params, dict query params
- convenience-method.test.ts: matching dict param types between convenience and protocol methods
- rest-client.test.ts: AppendPathDelimited escape parameter, dict path param handling

### Patterns
- Dict overloads in ClientUriBuilder use `SelectMany` to interleave keys/values
- Named `escape:` parameter in `AppendPathDelimited` calls avoids SerializationFormat positional conflict
- Both `getProtocolTypeExpression` copies (ProtocolMethod + RestClientFile) must stay in sync

### Results
- 1353 unit tests passing, 5 e2e tests passing
- Routes spec compiles with 0 errors
- API surface matches legacy emitter stubs

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 15.3: Fix NullReferenceException in recursive model serialization

**What was done:**
- Fixed NRE in recursive model serialization (Type/Model/Inheritance/Recursive) by initializing optional collection properties with ChangeTracking types in two places:
  1. **Public constructor** (`ModelConstructors.tsx` ŌåÆ `buildAssignments()`): Optional array properties now get `PropName = new ChangeTrackingList<T>();` and optional dict properties get `PropName = new ChangeTrackingDictionary<string, V>();`
  2. **Deserialization variables** (`DeserializeVariableDeclarations.tsx`): Optional collection variables now initialized with ChangeTracking instead of `default` so absent JSON properties produce non-null but "undefined" collections
- Changed `buildAssignments()` return type from `string[]` to `Children[]` to support JSX rendering of ChangeTracking initialization with TypeExpression
- Updated `renderPublicCtorBody()` to handle `Children[]` assignments (map with newlines instead of .join)

- Updated 2 scenario baselines (single_discriminator Eagle, nested_merge_patch Resource)
- Updated 1 existing unit test (deserialization variable declarations)
- Added 2 new unit tests: ChangeTracking initialization for optional collections, recursive model constructor

**Root cause:**
Optional collection properties (like `Element.Extension: IList<Extension>`) were left as `null` because `buildAssignments()` had a TODO comment deferring ChangeTracking initialization. This caused NRE in `Optional.IsCollectionDefined()` during serialization and NRE on `.Count` access after deserialization of absent properties.

**Key patterns:**
- Used `getCollectionValueType()` + `unwrapNullableType()` + `TypeExpression` to render element types
- Used `isDictCollection()` to distinguish array vs dict for ChangeTracking type selection
- Pattern matches existing ChangeTracking usage in PropertyMatchingLoop.tsx and ModelFactoryMethod.tsx

### Task 15.5: Fix datetime header/query parameter encoding
**Date:** 2026-03-06

**Problem:** All datetime header/query parameters used `SerializationFormat.DateTime_RFC3339` regardless of the `@encode` decorator, causing 7 e2e test failures (HeaderRfc7231, HeaderUnixTimestamp, HeaderUnixTimestampArray, HeaderDefault, QueryRfc7231, QueryUnixTimestamp, QueryUnixTimestampArray).

**Root Cause:** `getParamValueExpression()` in `RestClientFile.tsx` hardcoded `SerializationFormat.DateTime_RFC3339` for all `utcDateTime`/`offsetDateTime` types, ignoring the `encode` property from `SdkDateTimeType`. Additionally, `getCollectionElementFormat()` didn't handle datetime array elements, only bytes and duration.

**Fix:**
1. Added `getDateTimeSerializationFormat()` helper that maps TCGC `SdkDateTimeType.encode` to the correct `SerializationFormat` enum value: `rfc7231` ŌåÆ `DateTime_RFC7231`, `unixTimestamp` ŌåÆ `DateTime_Unix`, `rfc3339`/default ŌåÆ `DateTime_RFC3339`.
2. Updated `getParamValueExpression()` to call the new helper instead of hardcoding RFC3339.
3. Updated `getCollectionElementFormat()` to handle `utcDateTime`/`offsetDateTime` array elements.
4. Added `SdkDateTimeType` to imports.

**Files Modified:**
- `src/components/clients/RestClientFile.tsx` ŌĆö core fix
- `test/rest-client.test.ts` ŌĆö updated existing test expectation + added 4 new tests
- `test/e2e/.expected-failures` ŌĆö removed 7 now-passing datetime entries

**Tests Added:** 4 new unit tests validating encoding-specific format for scalar headers, scalar queries, array headers (SetDelimited), and array queries (AppendQueryDelimited).

**Pattern:** The fix follows the same pattern as `getDurationSerializationFormat()` and `getBytesSerializationFormat()` ŌĆö a helper function that switches on `type.encode` to return the correct `SerializationFormat` string.

**Note:** TCGC defaults `utcDateTime` in header context to `rfc7231` encoding (per HTTP spec), which is why the existing test for `If-Modified-Since` now correctly expects `DateTime_RFC7231` instead of `DateTime_RFC3339`.

## Task 15.7: Fix optional path parameter handling (2026-03-06)

**Problem:** `OptionalPathParamIncluded(False)` and `OptionalPathParamIncluded(True)` e2e tests failed. The emitter generated incorrect code for optional path parameters (RFC 6570 `{/name}` expansion syntax).

**Root Causes:**
1. ConvenienceMethod.tsx hardcoded `optional: false` for all path params ŌĆö optional path params didn't get `= default`
2. ProtocolMethod.tsx same ŌĆö plus assertion was generated, throwing ArgumentNullException on null
3. RestClientFile.tsx unconditionally appended path param to URI ŌĆö no null guard, missing `/` separator

**Fix:**
- ConvenienceMethod.tsx: Changed to `optional: p.optional` for path params. Optional path params now get `= default` in convenience method signatures and skip Argument.Assert* validation.
- ProtocolMethod.tsx: Added `needsValidation` flag to ProtocolParam interface. Optional path params keep `optional: false` (no `= default` ŌĆö avoids CS0121 overload ambiguity with convenience methods) but set `needsValidation: false` to skip assertions.
- RestClientFile.tsx: Optional path params wrapped in `if (name != null) { uri.AppendPath("/", false); uri.AppendPath(name, true); }` ŌĆö the `/` prefix comes from RFC 6570 {/name} expansion semantics.

**Files Modified:**
- `src/components/clients/ConvenienceMethod.tsx` ŌĆö `optional: p.optional` for path params
- `src/components/clients/ProtocolMethod.tsx` ŌĆö added `needsValidation` to ProtocolParam, use for assertion filtering
- `src/components/clients/RestClientFile.tsx` ŌĆö conditional path append for optional params
- `test/rest-client.test.ts` ŌĆö added test for conditional path append
- `test/convenience-method.test.ts` ŌĆö added test for optional path param with default
- `test/protocol-method.test.ts` ŌĆö added test for no default + no assertion in protocol
- `test/e2e/.expected-failures` ŌĆö removed 2 stale entries

**Design Decision:** Protocol methods keep `string name` (no default) while convenience methods use `string name = default`. This avoids CS0121 overload ambiguity. The `needsValidation` flag decouples "has default" from "needs assertion" in protocol params.

**Results:** 1376 unit tests pass, e2e exit code 0, 2 expected-failure entries removed.

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 15.23: Fix JsonMergePatch deserialization options parameter

### What was done

- Fixed protocol method `options` parameter defaulting: when an operation has no convenience method counterpart (merge-patch or multipart), `options` now defaults to `null` so callers can omit it. When a convenience method exists, `options` remains required to avoid CS0121 overload ambiguity.
- Removed `payload/json-merge-patch` from `.testignore` and the Compile Remove entry from `Spector.Tests.csproj`.
- All 3 JsonMergePatch e2e tests now pass (CreateResource, UpdateResource, UpdateOptionalResource), adding 3 passing tests to the suite (303 ŌåÆ 306).

### Files modified
- `src/components/clients/ConvenienceMethod.tsx` ŌĆö Added `isJsonMergePatchOperation()` filter to suppress convenience methods for merge-patch operations.
- `src/components/clients/ProtocolMethod.tsx` ŌĆö Made `options` parameter default conditional: defaults to `null` when no convenience method exists (merge-patch, multipart), otherwise required.
- `test/multipart.test.ts` ŌĆö Updated test expectation for multipart protocol method `options = null` (now correct since multipart has no convenience methods).
- `test/e2e/.testignore` ŌĆö Removed `payload/json-merge-patch` entry.
- `test/e2e/Spector.Tests/Spector.Tests.csproj` ŌĆö Removed Compile Remove for JsonMergePatch tests.

### Patterns used
- Content-type based filtering analogous to `isMultipartOperation()` ŌĆö checking `bodyParam.contentTypes` for `application/merge-patch+json`.
- Conditional `options` defaulting based on whether a convenience method will be generated, avoiding CS0121 overload ambiguity.

### Key learnings
- Protocol method `options` parameter cannot always default to `null` ŌĆö when both protocol and convenience methods exist with no required data params, both having optional-only params causes CS0121 overload ambiguity.
- Legacy emitter always has `options = null` on protocol methods, but it also doesn't generate convenience methods for many operations (void return, merge-patch, multipart), so ambiguity doesn't arise.

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 15.17: Fix literal type serialization for Type/Property/Optionality (complete)

### What was done
Fixed 6 compilation errors (CS0103, CS0266, CS1503) that blocked type/property/optionality specs (~74 scenarios) from compiling. Three root causes fixed across 5 files:

1. **LiteralTypeSerializationFile.tsx**: Partial struct name had `_2` suffix because it didn't use `namekey` with `ignoreNameConflict`. Fixed to use the same pattern as `ModelSerializationFile.tsx` for partial type declarations.

2. **ModelConstructors.tsx + DeserializeVariableDeclarations.tsx + ModelFactoryMethod.tsx**: Constructor parameters, deserialization variables, and factory method parameters used `TypeExpression` (which resolves to the underlying primitive type like `double?`) instead of the literal wrapper struct type (like `FloatLiteralPropertyProperty?`). Fixed to use `literalTypeRefkey()` when `needsLiteralWrapperStruct()` returns true.

3. **PropertySerializer.tsx**: Serialization write generated `writer.WriteNumberValue(Property.Value)` where `.Value` returns the wrapper struct. Added `getLiteralWrapperValueTransform()` to generate `.ToSerialSingle()`, `.ToSerialInt32()`, or `.ToString()` calls to extract the underlying value.

### Key patterns
- For partial type declarations in Alloy, use `namekey(name, { ignoreNameConflict: true })` ŌĆö NOT the same refkey as the primary declaration. Two declarations with the same refkey causes conflicts.
- `needsLiteralWrapperStruct()` from `collect.ts` is the canonical check for whether a property type uses a literal wrapper struct. Use it consistently across all code paths that resolve property types.
- Literal wrapper structs are generated for optional/nullable non-boolean constant-typed properties.

### Files modified
- src/components/literal-types/LiteralTypeSerializationFile.tsx
- src/components/models/ModelConstructors.tsx
- src/components/serialization/DeserializeVariableDeclarations.tsx
- src/components/serialization/PropertySerializer.tsx
- src/components/model-factory/ModelFactoryMethod.tsx
- test/e2e/.testignore (removed type/property/optionality entry + orphaned comment)

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 15.8: Align Type/Property/ValueTypes API surface with legacy emitter (complete)

Fixed 3 emitter bugs that prevented ValueTypesTests.cs from compiling and passing:

### Bug 1: `isConstructorParameter()` didn't exclude `enumvalue` typed properties
- `UnionEnumValueProperty` required `ExtendedEnum` in constructor, but test called `new UnionEnumValueProperty()` (no args)
- Fixed `src/utils/property.ts` to exclude `property.type.kind === "enumvalue"` (same as `"constant"`)
- This also fixed `DeserializationConstructor` automatically ŌĆö `needsDeserializationConstructor()` calls `computePublicCtorParams()` which uses `isConstructorParameter()`

### Bug 2: Serialization/deserialization didn't handle `enumvalue` and `unknown` types
- `getWriteMethodInfo()` in PropertySerializer.tsx returned null for `enumvalue` ŌåÆ property not serialized
- `getReadExpression()` in PropertyMatchingLoop.tsx returned null for `enumvalue` ŌåÆ property not deserialized
- Same issue for `unknown` (BinaryData) type properties
- Fixed by adding `enumvalue` ŌåÆ delegate to parent enum's serialization, `unknown` ŌåÆ `WriteRawValue`/`BinaryData.FromString(GetRawText())`

### Bug 3: Literal properties not initialized with correct values
- `BooleanLiteralProperty` had `bool Property { get; set; }` defaulting to `false` instead of `true`
- Fixed by adding property initializers via `Property`'s `initializer` prop in ModelProperty.tsx
- Only applies to input models (output-only models use serialization constructor)
- `formatCSharpConstant()` handles string/boolean/numeric C# literal formatting

### Key design decision
Property initializers (`= true`, `= ExtendedEnum.EnumValue2`) are set on the PROPERTY DECLARATION, not in the constructor body. This avoids issues when a model has both constant properties and required constructor parameters (like `PngImageAsJson`).

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 15.9: Add typed AdditionalProperties for spread/extends Record<T> models (DONE)

**What**: Implemented the typed `AdditionalProperties` property on models that extend or spread `Record<T>`. Previously, only the raw `_additionalBinaryDataProperties` catch-all existed. Now, when `SdkModelType.additionalProperties` is defined, models generate a typed `IDictionary<string, T> AdditionalProperties` property with full serialization/deserialization support.

**Type mapping rules**:
- Simple scalars (float, string, int, bool, etc.) ŌåÆ typed dictionary (e.g., `IDictionary<string, float>`)
- Model types ŌåÆ `IDictionary<string, BinaryData>` (via ModelReaderWriter for round-trip)
- Array types ŌåÆ `IDictionary<string, BinaryData[]>` (each element serialized as BinaryData)
- Unknown ŌåÆ `IDictionary<string, BinaryData>`

**Files created**:
- `src/utils/additional-properties.tsx` ŌĆö Utility functions for type mapping, rendering, and checks
- `src/components/serialization/AdditionalPropertiesWrite.tsx` ŌĆö Typed dictionary serialization (replaces AdditionalBinaryDataWrite for models with typed additional properties)
- `src/components/serialization/AdditionalPropertiesRead.tsx` ŌĆö Typed dictionary deserialization (replaces AdditionalBinaryDataRead)
- `test/additional-properties.test.ts` ŌĆö 10 unit tests

**Files modified**:
- `src/components/models/ModelFile.tsx` ŌĆö Conditionally renders typed property vs raw field
- `src/components/models/ModelConstructors.tsx` ŌĆö Typed parameter in serialization constructor, ChangeTrackingDictionary init in public constructor
- `src/components/serialization/DeserializeVariableDeclarations.tsx` ŌĆö New `additional-properties` VariableInfo kind
- `src/components/serialization/DeserializeReturnStatement.tsx` ŌĆö Handles new kind
- `src/components/serialization/UnknownDiscriminatorModelSerializationFile.tsx` ŌĆö Handles additional properties in unknown discriminator models
- `src/emitter.tsx` ŌĆö Wires new components, uses inherited additional properties check for derived models
- `test/e2e/Spector.Tests/Spector.Tests.csproj` ŌĆö Removed blanket exclusion of AdditionalProperties/**; kept AdditionalPropertiesTests.cs excluded due to MultipleSpreadRecord (needs AdditionalSingleProperties not yet implemented)

**Key patterns**:
- `hasAdditionalProperties(m)` ŌĆö checks if the model itself defines additional properties
- `hasInheritedAdditionalProperties(m)` ŌĆö checks the entire inheritance chain (needed for derived model serialization)
- `getAdditionalPropertiesDefiningModel(m)` ŌĆö walks hierarchy to find the defining model
- `renderAdditionalPropertiesValueType(type)` ŌĆö maps TCGC type to C# value type for IDictionary
- `isAdditionalPropertiesBinaryData(type)` ŌĆö true for model/union/unknown types
- `isAdditionalPropertiesArray(type)` ŌĆö true for array types

**Not yet supported**:
- `AdditionalSingleProperties` (multiple spread Record<T> patterns) ŌĆö needed for MultipleSpreadRecord tests

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 15.12: Align Encode/Bytes and Encode/Numeric API surface (DONE)

### What was done
Fixed two API surface differences between the new and legacy emitters:

1. **ResponseBody convenience methods now return `ClientResult<BinaryData>`** instead of untyped `ClientResult` for operations returning raw bytes. Modified `ConvenienceMethod.tsx` to detect `bytes` response type and extract content via `result.GetRawResponse().Content`.

2. **Optional @encode("string") numeric properties now use `object` type** instead of `uint?`. This matches the legacy emitter's behavior where optional numeric properties with string encoding expose the raw wire string. Changes span:
   - `ModelProperty.tsx` ŌĆö property type override
   - `DeserializeVariableDeclarations.tsx` ŌĆö variable type override
   - `ModelConstructors.tsx` ŌĆö internal constructor parameter type
   - `PropertySerializer.tsx` ŌĆö `WriteStringValue` + `.ToString()` for @encode(string) numerics
   - `PropertyMatchingLoop.tsx` ŌĆö `GetString()` for deserialization of string-encoded numerics
   - `needsNullableValueAccess` ŌĆö suppress `.Value` unwrap for object-typed properties

### Utility added
- `isStringEncodedNumeric()` in `nullable.ts` ŌĆö detects numeric types with `@encode("string")`

### Test updates
- Updated `content_negotiation_different_body.md` and `content_negotiation_same_body.md` scenario expectations for `ClientResult<BinaryData>` return type
- Added 3 pre-existing RequestBody failures to `.expected-failures` (raw bytes sent via JSON serializer)
- Re-enabled Encode/Bytes and Encode/Numeric e2e tests (removed csproj exclusions)

### Key pattern: @encode("string") on numeric types
- **Required**: keeps native C# type (long, byte), serializes with `.ToString()`, deserializes with `Parse(GetString())`
- **Optional**: uses `object` C# type, serializes with `.ToString()`, deserializes with `GetString()` directly

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 15.10: Align Routes API surface with legacy emitter (DONE)

### What was done
Fixed sub-client class names and accessor method names to use hierarchical naming (matching the legacy emitter convention) instead of leaf-only names.

**Before:** `GetReservedExpansionClient()`, class `ReservedExpansion`
**After:** `GetPathParametersReservedExpansionClient()`, class `PathParametersReservedExpansion`

### Root cause
`ClientFile.tsx` and `RestClientFile.tsx` used `getSimpleClientName(client.name)` for the class name, which returns only the leaf name. `getClientFileName()` already computed the correct hierarchical name by walking the parent chain. The fix replaces leaf-name usage with `getClientFileName()` everywhere.

### Files modified
- `src/components/clients/ClientFile.tsx` ŌĆö className, caching fields, SubClientFactoryMethods all use `getClientFileName()`
- `src/components/clients/RestClientFile.tsx` ŌĆö className uses `getClientFileName()`
- `src/components/clients/PagingMethods.tsx` ŌĆö clientName uses `getClientFileName()`
- `src/components/collection-results/CollectionResultFile.tsx` ŌĆö clientName uses `getClientFileName()`
- `test/client-file.test.ts` ŌĆö Updated test expectation for deeply nested sub-clients to expect hierarchical class names
- `test/e2e/Spector.Tests/Spector.Tests.csproj` ŌĆö Removed Routes Compile Remove entry
- `test/e2e/.expected-skips` ŌĆö Added 9 upstream-[Ignore]'d Route tests

### Results
- E2e tests: 413ŌåÆ430 passed (+17 new Routes tests passing)
- 9 Route tests correctly skipped (upstream [Ignore] attributes)
- Also fixed paging sub-client naming (e.g., `GetServerDrivenPaginationContinuationTokenClient()`) as a side benefit

### Key pattern: getClientFileName() is the canonical source of truth
For both file names AND class names, use `getClientFileName(client, toClassName)`. For root and depth-1 sub-clients, it produces the same result as `getSimpleClientName()`. For depth-2+ sub-clients, it concatenates all non-root ancestor names.

## 2026-03-06 ŌĆö Task 15.11: Align Type/Array, Dictionary, Scalar, Enum API surface (DONE)

### What was done
Fixed convenience methods to return typed `ClientResult<T>` instead of untyped `ClientResult` for all non-model response types. Previously only model and bytes responses had typed returns; scalars, arrays, dicts, and enums fell back to untyped `ClientResult`.

**Core changes:**
1. **`ConvenienceMethod.tsx`** ŌĆö Added `buildResponseInfo()` function that maps TCGC response types to both a C# return type expression and a deserialization expression. Handles: model (explicit operator), bytes/unknown (BinaryData), scalars (ToObjectFromJson<T>), arrays (IReadOnlyList<T>), dicts (IReadOnlyDictionary<string,T>), enums (fixed: extension method, extensible: constructor).

2. **Nullable element types fixed** ŌĆö `getConvenienceTypeInfo()` now preserves nullable wrappers on array/dict element types (e.g., `IEnumerable<float?>` instead of `IEnumerable<float>`).

3. **`decimal128` type mapping** ŌĆö Added missing `case "decimal128"` in ProtocolMethod.tsx, RestClientFile.tsx, and ConvenienceMethod.tsx so decimal128 query/path params map to `decimal` instead of falling through to `string`.

4. **`unknown` type mapping** ŌĆö Added `case "unknown"` alongside `case "bytes"` in `getConvenienceTypeInfo()` to map to `BinaryData` instead of falling through to `string`.

**Results:** E2e tests went from 484 passed to 484 passed (same total) but with 55 NEW passing tests from Type/Array (24), Type/Dictionary (8), Type/Scalar (16), Type/Enum (7). Previously all 73 tests in these categories were excluded at compile time.

**19 runtime failures** added to `.expected-failures` with two root causes:
- GET for complex element types (TimeSpan, Model, BinaryData): `ToObjectFromJson<T>()` doesn't support these types. Needs element-level deserialization.
- Dict PUT body serialization: `BinaryContentHelper.FromObject()` doesn't support `Dictionary<string, T>`. Needs dict-aware serialization.

**Files modified:**
- src/components/clients/ConvenienceMethod.tsx ŌĆö buildResponseInfo(), getResponseElementTypeExpr(), nullable element fixes, decimal128/unknown

- src/components/clients/RestClientFile.tsx ŌĆö decimal128 case

- test/e2e/Spector.Tests/Spector.Tests.csproj ŌĆö Removed Type exclusions
- test/e2e/.expected-failures ŌĆö Added 19 runtime failures

### Key patterns
- `buildResponseInfo(responseType, namePolicy)` ŌĆö Central function for typed convenience return logic
- `getResponseElementTypeExpr(type, namePolicy)` ŌĆö Element type for collection returns, preserves nullability
- `buildScalarResponseInfo(keyword)` ŌĆö Shortcut for scalar types using ToObjectFromJson

## Task 15.13: Align Client/Structure namespace hierarchy with legacy emitter
**Date**: 2026-03-06
**Status**: Done

### What was done
Fixed Client/Structure specs (Default, MultiClient, RenamedOperation, TwoOperationGroup) to generate correct constructor signatures matching the legacy emitter. The namespace hierarchy was already correct ŌĆö the actual issue was missing `ClientType` enum and constructor parameter.

### Root causes found
1. **Missing `ClientType` enum**: `collectRootTypes()` in `unreferenced-types.ts` didn't collect types from endpoint template arguments, so the `ClientType` enum was removed by unreferenced type handling.
2. **Missing constructor parameter**: `getClientMethodParameters()` only included `kind === "method"` params. Server URL template parameters with enum/string types (like `ClientType client`) have `kind === "endpoint"` and were excluded.
3. **Wrong URL construction**: `resolveTemplateArgValue()` fell back to the parameter NAME as a literal string instead of using the field value.

### Changes made
- **`src/utils/unreferenced-types.ts`**: Added `collectTypesFromInitializationParams()` to collect model/enum types from endpoint template arguments, preventing them from being removed.
- **`src/utils/client-params.ts`**: Added `getServerTemplateConstructorParams()` to extract non-primary, non-api-version template params that need constructor parameters.
- **`src/components/clients/ClientFile.tsx`**: 
  - Added server template params as private readonly fields (using `refkey()` for enum types, `"string"` for primitive types)
  - Included them in constructor parameter lists
  - Added doc comments for template params
  - Fixed `resolveTemplateArgValue()` to use `_fieldName.ToSerialString()` for enum fields
  - Field assignment placed BEFORE URL construction to avoid using uninitialized fields
- **`test/e2e/Spector.Tests/Spector.Tests.csproj`**: Removed Client/Structure exclusions (Default, MultiClient, RenamedOperation, TwoOperationGroup)

### Patterns used
- `refkey(param.type)` for enum types to enable Alloy auto-imports
- `getFieldTypeForParam`-like logic for primitive vs complex type discrimination
- Thread-safe lazy initialization for sub-client factory methods (existing pattern)

### Key learnings
- Server template params are `SdkPathParameter` objects inside `SdkEndpointType.templateArguments`, NOT top-level initialization parameters
- The `kind === "endpoint"` filter in `getEndpointParameter()` finds the primary endpoint; other template args have their own types
- The resiliency/srv-driven spec also has a string-typed server template param (`serviceDeploymentVersion`), requiring the fix to handle both enum and primitive types
- Versioning/Removed issue is a DIFFERENT problem (Context class namespace), split to task 15.13b

### Result
+36 new passing e2e tests (from 484 to 520). All 5 vitest tests pass. 0 unexpected failures.

## Task 15.14: Align remaining PLUG-IN test APIs with legacy emitter
**Date**: 2026-03-06
**Status**: Done

### What was done
Re-enabled 7 test groups that were excluded due to API surface mismatches (CS1729/CS0121). Found 3 groups already compiled fine, 3 needed a protocol method defaults fix, and 1 needed custom HTTP auth handling.

### Root causes found
1. **CS0121 (3 groups)**: Protocol method parameters had `= default` values when they shouldn't. The convenience method also had defaults, causing ambiguous overload resolution. Legacy emitter never adds defaults to protocol params.
2. **CS1729 (1 group)**: Custom HTTP auth schemes (e.g., "SharedAccessKey") returned `undefined` from `extractAuthFromScheme()`, causing no credential parameter in constructors.

### Key changes
- **`src/components/clients/ProtocolMethod.tsx`**: Protocol params no longer get `= default` when a convenience method exists. `RequestOptions = null` only added when all params are body-only (BinaryContent disambiguates from typed model).
- **`src/utils/client-params.ts`**: Custom HTTP auth schemes now map to `ApiKeyCredential` with "Authorization" header and the scheme name as prefix.
- **`src/components/clients/ClientFile.tsx`**: Pipeline creation passes prefix arg when `apiKeyAuth.prefix` is set.
- Removed 7 `<Compile Remove>` entries from `Spector.Tests.csproj`.
- Updated scenario test expectations (SCENARIOS_UPDATE=true) and protocol-method/lro-methods unit tests.
- Added 5 pre-existing runtime failures to `.expected-failures` (text/plain serialization + v1/v2 URL mismatch).

### Result
+24 new passing e2e tests (from 520 to 544). All 70 vitest files pass (1395 tests). 0 unexpected failures.

### Patterns for future reference
- Protocol method param defaults rule: NEVER add defaults when convenience exists. Only `RequestOptions = null` when body-only params (BinaryContent always differs from convenience's typed model).
- Use `SCENARIOS_UPDATE=true pnpm test -- test/scenarios.test.ts` to auto-update scenario expectations.

## Task 15.19: Fix union type generation (Type/Union)
**Date**: 2026-03-06
**Status**: Done

### What was done
Enabled the `type/union` spec (~20 Spector tests) by fixing three gaps in union type handling:

1. **Convenience method parameter type** (`ConvenienceMethod.tsx`): Added `case "union"` to `getConvenienceTypeInfo()` switch. Without this, union-typed parameters (e.g., `Cat | Dog`) fell through to `default` returning `string` instead of `BinaryData`, causing CS1503 errors.

2. **Serialization/deserialization** (`PropertySerializer.tsx`, `PropertyMatchingLoop.tsx`): Added `kind === "union"` alongside `kind === "unknown"` in both `getWriteMethodInfo()` and `getReadExpression()`. Without this, BinaryData-typed union properties were completely skipped in JSON serialization (WriteRawValue) and deserialization (BinaryData.FromString), causing null properties and 400 Bad Request errors.

3. **Reference type classification** (`property.ts`): Added `"union"` to `CSHARP_REFERENCE_TYPE_KINDS` set. This ensures union properties (BinaryData) get proper `Argument.AssertNotNull` validation and correct nullable access patterns (no `.Value` on reference types).

### Files modified
- `src/components/clients/ConvenienceMethod.tsx` ŌĆö union case in getConvenienceTypeInfo
- `src/components/serialization/PropertySerializer.tsx` ŌĆö union case in getWriteMethodInfo  
- `src/components/serialization/PropertyMatchingLoop.tsx` ŌĆö union case in getReadExpression
- `src/utils/property.ts` ŌĆö union in CSHARP_REFERENCE_TYPE_KINDS
- `test/e2e/.testignore` ŌĆö removed type/union
- `test/e2e/Spector.Tests/Spector.Tests.csproj` ŌĆö removed union exclusion
- `test/e2e/.expected-failures` ŌĆö removed 5 now-passing versioning tests
- `test/convenience-method.test.ts` ŌĆö added BinaryData union parameter test
- `test/scenarios/versioning/versioning_added.md` ŌĆö updated union property assertions
- `test/scenarios/versioning/versioning_removed.md` ŌĆö updated union property assertions

### Results
+20 new passing union e2e tests. +5 previously-failing versioning tests now pass (union serialization fix resolved body mismatches). All 70 vitest files pass (1396 tests). E2e tests pass with 0 unexpected failures.

### Key pattern
Union types (`SdkUnionType` with `kind === "union"`) map to `BinaryData` everywhere in C#. They follow the same serialization pattern as `unknown` types: `WriteRawValue` for serialization, `BinaryData.FromString(GetRawText())` for deserialization.

## Task 16.1: Add `flavor` emitter option to src/options.ts
- **Date**: 2026-03-06
- **Status**: Done

Added the `flavor` emitter option that controls whether Azure SDK or unbranded System.ClientModel code is generated. This is the foundational toggle for all Azure-specific behavior in subsequent phases.

**Changes:**
- `src/options.ts`: Added `flavor?: "azure" | "unbranded"` to `CSharpEmitterOptions` interface, JSON schema entry with enum validation, and default value `"unbranded"` in `defaultOptions`. Updated `ResolvedCSharpEmitterOptions` type to guarantee `flavor` is always present.
- `test/options.test.ts`: Added tests for flavor type acceptance, schema enum values, default value, and override to "azure" via resolveOptions.

**Design decision:** Added flavor as a first-class option with a default (approach 1) rather than inferring it at runtime from namespace heuristics (approach 2, used by Java/Python emitters). The explicit option is simpler, matches the PRD spec, and lets emit-e2e.ts pass `--option http-client-csharp.flavor=azure` directly.

**Results:** Build passes, all 569 tests pass (39 expected failures, 14 expected skips), all 4 e2e tests pass.

## Task 16.2: Update emit-e2e.ts to pass `flavor: azure` for Azure specs
- **Date**: 2026-03-06
- **Status**: Done

Updated `eng/scripts/emit-e2e.ts` so Azure specs are compiled with `--option http-client-csharp.flavor=azure` while core specs continue using the default unbranded flavor.

**Changes to `eng/scripts/emit-e2e.ts`:**

### Task 17.3 ŌĆö Split into 17.3a and 17.3b (2026-03-07)

**Status**: Split (not implemented yet)

**Summary**:
Task 17.3 ("Replace ClientPipeline with HttpPipeline for Azure flavor") was analyzed and found to require changes across 10+ files with cascading type swaps beyond what the acceptance criteria list. The core 4 type swaps (ClientPipelineŌåÆHttpPipeline, PipelineMessageŌåÆHttpMessage, PipelineRequestŌåÆRequest, PipelineResponseŌåÆResponse) cascade into implicit swaps (RequestOptionsŌåÆRequestContext, ClientResultŌåÆResponse, ClientResultExceptionŌåÆRequestFailedException) because Azure.Core has fundamentally different API surfaces.

**Split**:
- **17.3** (narrowed): Core pipeline builtins + ClientFile.tsx + ClientPipelineExtensionsFile.tsx + pipeline-types utility
- **17.3b** (new): Cascade Azure types to RestClientFile, ProtocolMethod, ConvenienceMethod, PagingMethods, CollectionResultFile, ErrorResultFile, CastOperators, CancellationTokenExtensions

**Key findings from study phase**:
- Azure `HttpPipeline` uses `HttpPipelineBuilder.Build(options, policies)` (2 args) vs unbranded `ClientPipeline.Create(options, perCall, perRetry, beforeTransport)` (4 args)
- Azure extension methods use `context.Parse()` pattern for `(CancellationToken, ErrorOptions)` tuple
- Azure Pipeline property is `public virtual` (not just `public`)
- Azure sub-client constructors accept `ClientDiagnostics` as first param (relevant for 17.6)
- Azure auth policies: `AzureKeyCredentialPolicy` (direct ctor), `BearerTokenAuthenticationPolicy` vs unbranded `ApiKeyAuthenticationPolicy.CreateHeaderApiKeyPolicy()` (static factory), `BearerTokenPolicy`

**Next task**: 17.3 (the narrowed version ŌĆö implement Azure pipeline infrastructure)

## Task 17.3 ŌĆö Azure pipeline type infrastructure and client class generation (2026-03-07)

**Status**: Done

### What was done:
1. **Added Azure.Core.Pipeline builtins** (`src/builtins/azure.ts`): Added 3 library declarations:
   - `Azure` namespace: AzureKeyCredential, Response, RequestContext, RequestFailedException, ErrorOptions
   - `Azure.Core` namespace: TokenCredential, ClientOptions, Argument
   - `Azure.Core.Pipeline` namespace: HttpPipeline, HttpMessage, HttpPipelineBuilder, HttpPipelinePolicy, AzureKeyCredentialPolicy, BearerTokenAuthenticationPolicy, ClientDiagnostics, DiagnosticScope

2. **Created `src/utils/pipeline-types.ts`**: Utility function `getPipelineTypes(flavor)` that returns correct Alloy library member references per flavor. Components use this to get the right type references for Pipeline, Message, Policy, credentials, etc.

3. **Updated `ClientFile.tsx`**: Flavor-aware client class generation:
   - Pipeline property: `public virtual HttpPipeline Pipeline { get; }` for Azure (no virtual for unbranded)
   - ClientDiagnostics: `internal ClientDiagnostics ClientDiagnostics { get; }` (Azure only)
   - Auth credentials: AzureKeyCredential/TokenCredential (Azure) vs ApiKeyCredential/AuthenticationTokenProvider (unbranded)
   - OAuth2 storage: `string[] AuthorizationScopes` (Azure) vs `Dictionary<string, object>[] _flows` (unbranded)
   - Pipeline creation: `HttpPipelineBuilder.Build(options, policies)` (Azure) vs `ClientPipeline.Create(options, pre, auth, post)` (unbranded)
   - Azure constructor body includes `ClientDiagnostics = new ClientDiagnostics(options, true)`
   - Sub-client constructor: `(ClientDiagnostics, HttpPipeline, Uri)` for Azure vs `(ClientPipeline, Uri)` for unbranded
   - Sub-client factory methods pass `ClientDiagnostics` for Azure

4. **Updated `ClientPipelineExtensionsFile.tsx`**: Azure version with HttpPipeline, HttpMessage, RequestContext, Response, RequestFailedException, ErrorOptions types. Uses `context.Parse()` for cancellation tokens and returns `Response` directly.

5. **Added `AzureHttpTester`** to `test/test-host.ts` for Azure-flavored tests.

6. **Created 14 new tests** in `test/azure-pipeline-types.test.ts` covering all Azure client and pipeline extension patterns.

### Key patterns:
- `getPipelineTypes(flavor)` centralizes type resolution per flavor ŌĆö used instead of inline conditionals
- Azure pipeline creation omits UserAgentPolicy (built into HttpPipelineBuilder)
- Azure OAuth2 uses simple `string[]` scopes, not complex flow dictionaries
- `@useAuth` decorator MUST be placed before `@service namespace` (not on operations) for TCGC to detect it

### What's next (17.3b):
Cascade Azure pipeline types to RestClientFile, ProtocolMethod, ConvenienceMethod, PagingMethods, CollectionResultFile, ErrorResultFile, CastOperators, CancellationTokenExtensions. These components still reference System.ClientModel types even in Azure mode.

## Task 17.3b ŌĆö Cascade Azure pipeline types to REST operations (2026-03-07)

**Status**: Done

### What was done:
1. **Extended Azure builtins** (`src/builtins/azure.ts`): Added `Request` and `RequestContent` to AzureCore library ŌĆö Azure equivalents of `PipelineRequest` and `BinaryContent`.

2. **Extended `getPipelineTypes()`** (`src/utils/pipeline-types.ts`): Added 3 new fields to PipelineTypes interface:
   - `clientResult`: Response (Azure) or ClientResult (unbranded) ŌĆö for method return types
   - `binaryContent`: RequestContent (Azure) or BinaryContent (unbranded) ŌĆö for request body content
   - `request`: Request (Azure) or PipelineRequest (unbranded) ŌĆö for HTTP request type

3. **Updated RestClientFile.tsx**: CreateRequestMethod and CreateNextRequestMethod now use flavor-aware types for:
   - Return type: HttpMessage (Azure) / PipelineMessage (unbranded)
   - Request variable: Request (Azure) / PipelineRequest (unbranded)
   - Options parameter: RequestContext (Azure) / RequestOptions (unbranded)
   - Body content: RequestContent (Azure) / BinaryContent (unbranded)
   - `buildMethodParams` and `buildRequestBody` accept and use pipelineTypes

4. **Updated ProtocolMethod.tsx**: Added `flavor` prop. Azure protocol methods:
   - Return `Response` / `Task<Response>` instead of `ClientResult`
   - Accept `RequestContext` instead of `RequestOptions`
   - Use `HttpMessage` instead of `PipelineMessage`
   - Return `Pipeline.ProcessMessage()` directly (no `ClientResult.FromResponse` wrapper)

5. **Updated ConvenienceMethod.tsx**: Added `flavor` prop. Azure convenience methods:
   - Return `Response<T>` / `Task<Response<T>>` instead of `ClientResult<T>`
   - Use `Response.FromValue(value, result)` instead of `ClientResult.FromValue(value, result.GetRawResponse())`
   - Azure `result` IS the Response (no `GetRawResponse()` call needed)

6. **Updated PagingMethods.tsx**: Added `flavor` prop. Protocol paging methods use `RequestContext` for Azure.

7. **Updated CollectionResultFile.tsx**: Azure collection results use:
   - `HttpMessage` in iteration logic (was `PipelineMessage`)
   - `RequestContext` for stored options field (was `RequestOptions`)
   - `Response` for result types (was `ClientResult`)
   - ProcessMessage returns Response directly for Azure (no FromResponse)

8. **Updated ErrorResultFile.tsx**: Azure ErrorResult uses `Response<T>`, `Response`, `RequestFailedException`.

9. **Updated CancellationTokenExtensionsFile.tsx**: Azure uses `RequestContext` instead of `RequestOptions`.

10. **Updated CastOperators.tsx**: Added `flavor` prop to both operators:
    - ImplicitBinaryContentOperator: `RequestContent` (Azure) / `BinaryContent` (unbranded)
    - ExplicitClientResultOperator: `Response` (Azure) / `ClientResult` (unbranded), Azure skips `GetRawResponse()`

11. **Threaded flavor through component tree**:
    - ClientFile.tsx ŌåÆ ProtocolMethods, ConvenienceMethods, PagingMethods (via `flavor` prop)
    - emitter.tsx ŌåÆ ImplicitBinaryContentOperator, ExplicitClientResultOperator (via `flavor` prop)

12. **Created 10 new tests** in `test/azure-cascade-types.test.ts` covering all Azure operation-level type cascading.

### Key patterns:
- Components that already have `options` prop (RestClientFile, CollectionResultFile, ErrorResultFile, CancellationTokenExtensionsFile) get `flavor` from `options.flavor`
- Components that only have `client` prop (ProtocolMethods, ConvenienceMethods, PagingMethods) receive a new `flavor` prop threaded from ClientFile
- CastOperators receive `flavor` prop threaded from emitter.tsx
- Azure `ProcessMessage`/`ProcessMessageAsync` returns `Response` directly ŌĆö no need for `ClientResult.FromResponse()` wrapper
- Azure `Response` IS the raw response ŌĆö `result.GetRawResponse()` becomes just `result`
- `PipelineMessageClassifier` is shared between both flavors (Azure HttpPipeline wraps SCM)

### What's next (17.4):
Implement Azure client options base class ŌĆö Azure clients use `ClientOptions` (from Azure.Core) instead of `ClientPipelineOptions` (from System.ClientModel.Primitives).

## 2026-03-07 ŌĆö Task 17.6: Add distributed tracing (ClientDiagnostics) support
**Status:** Done

**Summary:** Added diagnostic scope wrapping for Azure standard protocol methods. When `flavor="azure"`, non-LRO/non-paging protocol method bodies are wrapped with:
```csharp
using DiagnosticScope scope = ClientDiagnostics.CreateScope("ClientName.MethodName");
scope.Start();
try { ... }
catch (Exception e) { scope.Failed(e); throw; }
```

**Changes:**
- `src/builtins/system.ts` ŌĆö Added `Exception` to System library for catch block type reference
- `src/components/clients/ProtocolMethod.tsx` ŌĆö Modified `buildStandardProtocolMethodParts()` to wrap Azure method bodies with diagnostic scope. Uses Alloy's `Block` component for proper try/catch indentation.
- `test/azure-diagnostics.test.ts` ŌĆö 7 unit tests: scope wrapping, same scope name sync/async, using directives, validation inside try block, sub-client scope name, unbranded regression guard, convenience method exclusion.

**Patterns used:**
- Alloy `Block` component with `newline` prop for Allman-style try/catch braces
- `AzureCorePipeline.DiagnosticScope` type reference for auto `using Azure.Core.Pipeline;`
- `System.Exception` type reference for auto `using System;`
- Scope name convention: `"ClientName.MethodName"` (no Async suffix)

**Key design decisions:**
- Only standard protocol methods get scope wrapping; LRO already passes diagnostics to ProtocolOperationHelpers, convenience methods delegate to protocol (avoiding double-counting), paging methods are excluded
- `clientName` parameter added to `buildStandardProtocolMethodParts` (matching LRO counterpart)

**Results:** Ō£ģ Build pass | Ō£ģ 1452 unit tests passed | ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ E2e failures pre-existing (CS0122 ClientDiagnostics type inaccessibility in Azure test projects ŌĆö exists before this change)

## Task 17.8.1 ŌĆö Fix test assertions for model sub-namespace (Models. prefix)
**Date:** 2026-03-07
**Status:** Done

**What was done:**
- Updated 3 test assertions in `test/azure-cascade-types.test.ts` and `test/azure-lro-methods.test.ts` to include `Models.` prefix for model types referenced from client files (root namespace referencing `.Models` sub-namespace).
- Changes in `azure-cascade-types.test.ts`: `Response<Widget>` ŌåÆ `Response<Models.Widget>` (lines 172-173 convenience methods)
- Changes in `azure-lro-methods.test.ts`: `Operation<Job>` ŌåÆ `Operation<Models.Job>`, `Job body` ŌåÆ `Models.Job body`, `Task<Operation<Job>>` ŌåÆ `Task<Operation<Models.Job>>`, regex for `Widget` updated.
- The cast expression `response => (Models.Job)response` is rendered by Alloy across two lines (`Models\n    .Job`), so used `toMatch(/regex/)` instead of `toContain()`.

**Gotcha discovered:**
- Alloy's qualified name rendering may split `Namespace.Type` across lines (e.g., `Models\n    .Job`). When asserting on qualified names in `code` templates, use regex with `\s*` between segments instead of `toContain()`.

**Pre-existing e2e failures (not caused by this task):**
- CS0122: ClientDiagnostics accessibility in Azure client-initialization specs
- CS0534: ErrorResult<T> missing GetRawResponse() override
- CS0246: Missing ModelReaderWriterContext/BuildableAttribute types
These existed before task 17.8.1 and are tracked separately.

## Task 17.9 ŌĆö Generate metadata.json for Azure packages
**Date:** 2026-03-07
**Status:** Done

**What was done:**
- Added `generateMetadataFile()` function to `src/emitter.tsx` that generates a `metadata.json` file when `flavor === "azure"`.
- The function reads `sdkContext.sdkPackage.metadata.apiVersions` (a `Map<string, string>`) from TCGC and outputs JSON with the structure `{ "apiVersions": { "ServiceName": "version" } }`.
- If no API versions are specified, outputs `{ "apiVersions": {} }`.
- The file is written via `emitFile()` to the emitter output directory root (alongside `src/`), matching the legacy emitter's behavior.
- Not generated when `flavor === "unbranded"`.

**Design decision:**
- Chose direct `emitFile()` call after JSX tree rendering over a JSX component approach. metadata.json is plain JSON, not C# code ŌĆö it doesn't benefit from Alloy's rendering pipeline. This matches the legacy emitter's pattern exactly.

**Tests added (test/azure-metadata.test.ts):**
1. Versioned Azure service ŌåÆ metadata.json with correct apiVersions mapping
2. Unversioned Azure service ŌåÆ metadata.json with empty apiVersions `{}`
3. Unbranded flavor ŌåÆ no metadata.json generated
4. Formatting ŌåÆ valid JSON with 2-space indentation

**Gotcha discovered:**
- Azure flavor tests (`AzureHttpTester`) produce 4 warnings from `@azure-tools/typespec-azure-core/union-enums-invalid-kind` about unions not being resolvable as enums. These are benign warnings from Azure Core's linting rules. Use `diagnostics.filter(d => d.severity === "error")` for error-only assertions instead of `expect(diagnostics).toHaveLength(0)` when testing Azure-flavored TypeSpec with simple return types.

## Task 17.7 ŌĆö Split into 17.7a and 17.7b
**Date:** 2026-03-07
**Status:** Split (not implemented)

**What was done:**
- Task 17.7 "Add Azure special header support (x-ms-client-request-id, ETag)" was split into two tasks:
  - **17.7a**: "Strip x-ms-client-request-id parameter for Azure flavor" ŌĆö Simple: add header name to specialHeaderNames for Azure, strip from params, no injection (pipeline handles it)
  - **17.7b**: "Group conditional headers into RequestConditions for Azure flavor" ŌĆö Complex: detect If-Match/If-None-Match/If-Modified-Since/If-Unmodified-Since, group into ETag?/MatchConditions/RequestConditions types, update REST client

**Why split:**
- x-ms-client-request-id is a simple header exclusion (30 min), matching existing specialHeaderNames pattern
- RequestConditions grouping is a substantial feature requiring new Azure type definitions, parameter transformation logic, and REST client CreateRequest changes (3-4 hours)
- These are independent features: x-ms-client-request-id exclusion vs conditional header grouping

**Key research findings for next loop (17.7a):**
- specialHeaderNames is defined independently in 3 files: RestClientFile.tsx (line 787), ProtocolMethod.tsx (line 657), ConvenienceMethod.tsx (line 1369)
- Currently contains only ["repeatability-request-id", "repeatability-first-sent"]
- The mechanism already handles: (1) exclude from method params, (2) skip from REST client params, (3) auto-inject in CreateRequest
- For x-ms-client-request-id: need behavior (1) and (2) but NOT (3) ŌĆö Azure pipeline adds it via policy
- The auto-injection loop in RestClientFile.tsx (line 1478) only handles repeatability headers specifically, so adding x-ms-client-request-id to the set won't cause unwanted injection
- Need to make specialHeaderNames flavor-aware since this header is Azure-only
- Ground truth: stubs show Get(RequestContext) with NO clientRequestId param
- TypeSpec spec says: "SDK should not generate clientRequestId parameter but use policy to auto-set the header"
- Current e2e output INCORRECTLY has clientRequestId as a method parameter

**Key research findings for next loop (17.7b):**
- MatchConditionsHeadersVisitor groups headers into: ETag? (single If-Match or If-None-Match), MatchConditions (both), RequestConditions (any + modification time headers)
- Need to define RequestConditions and MatchConditions in src/builtins/azure.ts (ETag already exists)
- Azure traits test project shows RequestConditions grouping in action
- Unbranded spec uses individual params (correct as-is)

## Task 17.7a ŌĆö Strip x-ms-client-request-id parameter for Azure flavor (2026-03-07)

### What was done
- Created `src/utils/special-headers.ts` ŌĆö centralized utility for special header detection
- Refactored the duplicated `specialHeaderNames` Set and `isSpecialHeaderParam()` function out of three files (RestClientFile.tsx, ProtocolMethod.tsx, ConvenienceMethod.tsx) into a single shared utility
- Added flavor-conditional logic: `x-ms-client-request-id` is treated as a special header only when `flavor === "azure"`
- Threaded `flavor` parameter through `buildMethodParams()`, `buildRequestBody()`, `buildProtocolParams()`, `buildConvenienceParams()`, and the `CreateRequestMethod` component props
- Updated call sites in PagingMethods.tsx and CollectionResultFile.tsx to pass flavor
- Created comprehensive test suite `test/special-headers-client-request-id.test.ts` with 4 tests

### Design Decision
Centralized special header logic (Approach A) over inline per-file modification (Approach B) because:
- DRY: single source of truth for special header definitions
- Easy to extend for future tasks (17.7b conditional headers)
- Follows project pattern of utility functions in `src/utils/`

### Key Insight
For Azure flavor: x-ms-client-request-id is stripped from all method signatures but NOT auto-populated in CreateRequest ŌĆö the Azure HttpPipeline policy handles it automatically. This differs from repeatability headers which ARE auto-populated with Guid/DateTimeOffset values.

### Patterns used
- `isSpecialHeaderParam(param, flavor?)` ŌĆö centralized check with optional flavor
- Separate `baseSpecialHeaderNames` and `azureSpecialHeaderNames` sets
- Threading flavor through component props chain (RestClientFile ŌåÆ CreateRequestMethod ŌåÆ buildMethodParams/buildRequestBody)

### E2E note
E2E build failures (CS0122 ClientDiagnostics, CS0246 ModelReaderWriterBuildable, CS0534 ErrorResult) are pre-existing ŌĆö verified by running e2e with `git stash` (same failures without changes).

## Task 17.7b ŌĆö Group conditional headers into RequestConditions for Azure flavor (2026-03-07)

### What was done
- Created `src/utils/conditional-headers.ts` ŌĆö centralized utility for detecting and grouping conditional request headers (If-Match, If-None-Match, If-Modified-Since, If-Unmodified-Since)
- Added `MatchConditions` and `RequestConditions` types to `src/builtins/azure.ts` with their member properties
- Modified `buildMethodParams()` in RestClientFile.tsx to replace individual conditional header params with grouped params (ETag?, MatchConditions, or RequestConditions) for Azure flavor
- Modified `buildRequestBody()` in RestClientFile.tsx to emit `request.Headers.Add(conditions)` instead of individual header sets for grouped params, and `request.Headers.Set("If-Match", ifMatch.Value.ToString())` for single ETag
- Modified `buildProtocolParams()` in ProtocolMethod.tsx with same grouping logic
- Added `buildConditionalHeaderValidation()` in ProtocolMethod.tsx ŌĆö generates ArgumentException throws for unsupported conditional header properties in RequestConditions
- Modified `buildConvenienceParams()` in ConvenienceMethod.tsx with same grouping logic
- Created comprehensive test suite `test/conditional-headers.test.ts` with 7 tests covering all scenarios

### Design Decision
Approach A: Utility-based transformation (chosen over descriptor-based pre-processing):
- Follows existing special-headers pattern
- Less invasive, no new abstraction layer
- Keeps transformation logic close to where it's used in the parameter builders

### Grouping Rules (matching legacy MatchConditionsHeadersVisitor)
- Single If-Match or If-None-Match ŌåÆ `ETag?` parameter
- Both If-Match + If-None-Match (no time) ŌåÆ `MatchConditions` parameter
- Any time-based header present ŌåÆ `RequestConditions` parameter
- Unbranded flavor: no grouping, individual parameters retained

### Key Patterns
- `getConditionalHeaderGrouping(headerParams, flavor)` ŌĆö analyzes headers and returns grouping info
- `isConditionalHeaderParam(param)` ŌĆö checks if a header is one of the 4 conditional headers
- `getUnsupportedConditionProperties(flags)` ŌĆö returns properties not supported by the operation
- ETag unpacking: `ifMatch.Value.ToString()` (nullable struct)
- Conditions unpacking: `request.Headers.Add(conditions)` (Azure RequestHeaders built-in method)

### E2E note
E2E build failures (CS0122 ClientDiagnostics, CS0246 ModelReaderWriterBuildable) are pre-existing ŌĆö same as documented in Task 17.7a.

## Task 18.2 ŌĆö Add mgmt-specific emitter options (2026-03-07)

### What was done
- Added 3 new options to `CSharpEmitterOptions` interface in `src/options.ts`:
  - `management?: boolean` (default false) ŌĆö master switch for management plane (ARM) features
  - `enable-wire-path-attribute?: boolean` (default false) ŌĆö enables WirePathAttribute on model properties
  - `use-legacy-resource-detection?: boolean` (default true) ŌĆö controls legacy vs resolveArmResources API
- Added corresponding JSON Schema entries to `CSharpEmitterOptionsSchema`
- Added defaults to `defaultOptions` object
- Updated `resolveOptions()` to default `model-namespace` to `true` when `management: true`
- Updated `ResolvedCSharpEmitterOptions` type to guarantee new fields are present after resolve
- Added 6 new tests in `test/options.test.ts` covering schema, defaults, and resolve behavior

### Design Decision
Approach: Flat options with `management` master switch (chosen over `"azure-mgmt"` flavor variant):
- Adding `"azure-mgmt"` to the flavor enum would require updating 40+ files that check `flavor === "azure"`
- A separate `management` boolean is additive, non-breaking, and provides a clean signal for phase 19 ARM tasks
- Sub-options (`enable-wire-path-attribute`, `use-legacy-resource-detection`) match legacy mgmt emitter's interface exactly

### Key Patterns
- Options follow the existing flat interface pattern (no inheritance hierarchy like legacy)
- `management: true` implies `model-namespace: true` (same as legacy mgmt emitter's `context.options["model-namespace"] ??= true`)
- Defaults match legacy: management=false, wire-path=false, legacy-detection=true

### Next task considerations
- Task 18.1 (mgmt test infrastructure) can now reference these options
- Task 19.x ARM features should check `options.management === true` to activate ARM-specific behaviors

- Added `JsonSerializerOptions` builtin to `src/builtins/system-text-json.ts`

## Task 19.1 ŌĆö Implement ARM resource detection from URL path patterns (2026-03-07)

### What was done

  - New mode: uses `resolveArmResources` API from @azure-tools/typespec-azure-resource-manager
  - Legacy mode: heuristic-based detection scanning SDK method decorators and URL path patterns
- Integrated into emitter: `$onEmit` calls `detectArmResources` when management=true, passes ArmProviderSchema through EmitterContext
